in: Article stubs, KQC2, Transcripts, KQAOG transcripts

KQC2 transcript

Sign in to edit
  • History
  • Purge
  • Talk (0)
This article is a stub. You can help King's Quest Omnipedia by expanding it.
 

The KQC2 transcript contains the various scripts for the characters in King's Quest Chapter II: Rubble Without a Cause. There is quite a bit of material that was from the released game, that can be read in the game script.

Noteably absent from the game are the parts for Whisper and Acorn[1], but there is additional stuff for many of the other characters that appear to be related to removed areas, puzzles, or events (including the 'companion' system appears to have once been planned to have been a bit more dynamic and used for more than one puzzle). The unused material may make up half of the script material.
